    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

  <span id="freeText11998904188162396370" style="display:none">Done with being the world's biggest pushover, Haley decides that things are going to change starting with the aggravating neighbor who has too much charm and not enough restraint. What she didn't expect was to be sucked into his world, but Haley has a game plan and she won't let herself forget just what the bad boy next door is capable of.<br /><br />The last thing Jason expected was for his little shy neighbor to go Rambo on him over some ruined flowers. After he decides to take her under his wing he can't help but that notice that she fits very nicely in his life. Now the only thing left is to convince her that this is anything but a game.<br /><br /><br /><br />©2011 R.L. Mathewson</span>

<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/299063-would-this-book-be-inappropriate-for-an">Would this book be inappropriate for an 8th grader?</a>
</div>
<div class='communityQAFooter questionFooter'>
<ul class='questionFooterActions'>
<li class='footerItem like'>
<span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_community_question_299063'><a id="like_count_community_question_299063" rel="nofollow" href="/rating/voters/299063?resource_type=CommunityQuestion"><span class="likesCount">2 likes</span></a>&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;<a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F11381643-playing-for-keeps">like</a></span>

</li>
<li class='footerItem communityQuestionTimestamp'>
<a href="/questions/299063-would-this-book-be-inappropriate-for-an">5 years ago</a>
</li>
<li class='footerItem communityQuestionPermalink'>
<a href="/questions/299063-would-this-book-be-inappropriate-for-an">See all 6 answers</a>
</li>
</ul>
</div>

</div>
<div class='allCommunityAnswers'>
<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/33401229-jen-lynn"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1437423682i/33401229._UY100_CR39,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/33401229-jen-lynn">Jen Lynn</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Ma gawd yes. Psh. If you're mature enough to look at the book and probably already know the book's context is mature adult; than I would say the heck <a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Ma gawd yes. Psh. If you're mature enough to look at the book and probably already know the book's context is mature adult; than I would say the heck at it. It's just a book. I read stuff like this in the 8th grade as well. It all depends on you're maturity level. But really it's all up to you. No one's gonna get on you're back if you want to read a book. Just read a few chapters and if it's for you than go ahead and read it. If it's not than choose something else. Helpful hint; Try typing in Mature YA novels on Goodreads or Google and there's a whole list for more of young adult age groups who don't mind explicit scenes and other mature topics. I know where you're coming from. I feel like I've already read a lot of the YA novels such as sunshine state and they just bore me to death. I mean it's just books and sometimes we can learn a lot from reading mature books. There's more lessons to gather and experiences that might help us when we grow up more. In my opinion. But if you're old enough to look book like these up and find them interesting than certainly your old enough to read the book. I can handle some non-mature books though as well. Such as Hush, Hush series and the Obsidian series, ect. They both have a good love-hate relationship with angels and than Aliens.(Sounds horny but they're good reads.) You've probably already read it though. C.C Enjoy reading... it's all about what you enjoy. And if you enjoy this stuff(Like me) than I say go for it! (Little late for answering this but yah know.) C=<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>
</div>

<span id="freeTextContainer16627364000304165957">Sometimes when I read other people's reviews, I think "Did we read the same book?"<br/><br/>Anyways, the good- this book is very well written, esp by the standards of self pubs. It flows well and is very engaging. I had fun while I was reading it and kept turning the pages. It really lost me in the last third though.<br/><br/>The bad- this book is about two idiot adult children who take immaturity to a new level. Hayley starts dating her neighbor Jason when they are trapped inside her house by a swarm of killer bee</span>
  <span id="freeText16627364000304165957" style="display:none">Sometimes when I read other people's reviews, I think "Did we read the same book?"<br /><br />Anyways, the good- this book is very well written, esp by the standards of self pubs. It flows well and is very engaging. I had fun while I was reading it and kept turning the pages. It really lost me in the last third though.<br /><br />The bad- this book is about two idiot adult children who take immaturity to a new level. Hayley starts dating her neighbor Jason when they are trapped inside her house by a swarm of killer bees. They hit it off and start hanging out as "just friends" for several months, a relationship that soon includes tons of platonic sleeping. Before long, they can't sleep alone. Jason wants to fuck Hayley, but he is sure that she would never want to be with a man like him. If there are any men reading this, here is a hint- if a woman lets you sleep in her bed every night for three months, then she is probably also willing to fuck you. I'm just saying. <br /><br />However, the real reason that Haley hasn't sealed the deal is because she is a virgin and saving herself for the man she loves. However, even though she isn't sure she loves Jason, she sure likes him a lot, so they begin an epic months long spree of oral sex that lasts like 200 pages. Luckily for Hayley, Jason enjoys eating pussy more than a JR Ward vampire crossed with Lil Wayne crossed with Cookie Monster. There is trouble in paradise though, when one of her asshole friends tricks Jason into doing the horizontal polka before Hayley is ready. Haley is hurt and tries to dump Jason but he just won't take no for an answer. In his defense, I don't think that I would assume that a 30 year old woman would be a virgin either. Through the power of forgivness and buttercream frosting, they get over it.<br /><br />Anyways, what kills me about this story is that there should have been no story. Two unattached, normal consenting adults shouldn't have had this much trouble. Just not enough conflict outside the characters unexplained immaturity. Jason especially was hard for me to figure out.<br /><br />However, this book does contain several things that seem to be trends in new romance novels, including platonic sleeping, animal nicknames and an extremely long epilogue. All of these things piss me off, especially the platonic sleeping. If you like it though, good for you. I would rather read about real adults.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16627364000304165957" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText1821315529983609110" style="display:none"><b>O.M.G.! What a funny and sexy contemporary romance! </b> It was over-the-top silly, but it made me laugh so many times! And best yet, the steamy parts were HOT. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380369054i/721730.jpg" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jason is Haley’s next door neighbor from HELL, but in truth he really is a fun and misunderstood kind of guy. Sure, the neighborhood started <s>a few</s> many petitions trying to get him to stop doing this or that, but he means well. And his shy little neighbor has never once complained. However, Jason is pretty clueless when it comes to things like women. Lucky for him, Haley is a great teacher. <br><br>Zachary Knighton as Jason:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380369054i/721731.jpg" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Shy school teacher Haley can’t believe she finally stood up for herself against the jerk neighbor, but it felt good. It was funny, hot and just what I was in the mood for. While Jason was a bit full of himself, I found myself really enjoying his character. Haley was a perfect fit for a guy like him, and it was fun watching her deal with her shyness. My only complaint is that I felt the laughs faded too much toward the end as Jason and Haley had to work through their drama before they could find their own HEA. Still, I really enjoyed it and I'll be reading more of this series. Thanks to all my Goodreads friends who recommended this, otherwise I probably would never have found it on my own. <br><br></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jill Paige" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jill Paige" href="/user/show/11083878-jill-paige">Jill Paige</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer371938766" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10223152208532372568">Unfortunately, I only got to page 39 of this book before I gave up on it. <br/><br/>The blurb implies it's a enemies-to-lovers trope, but the hero and heroine are only enemies for (literally) the first pages of the book. Very soon they're instant best friends--which we are TOLD, not shown--so the book is really a friends-to-lovers trope.<br/><br/>The friends-to-lovers trope wouldn't have put me off, but adding to the book's woes, it was poorly edited. (I have since read that the author is having her books edited AF</span>
  <span id="freeText10223152208532372568" style="display:none">Unfortunately, I only got to page 39 of this book before I gave up on it. <br /><br />The blurb implies it's a enemies-to-lovers trope, but the hero and heroine are only enemies for (literally) the first pages of the book. Very soon they're instant best friends--which we are TOLD, not shown--so the book is really a friends-to-lovers trope.<br /><br />The friends-to-lovers trope wouldn't have put me off, but adding to the book's woes, it was poorly edited. (I have since read that the author is having her books edited AFTER their release).<br /><br />Again, these two things would not necessarily have been deal breakers for me. Unfortunately, the hero (Jason) was. Jason takes an entire plate of cookies and refuses to share them with anybody. When he learns there is a second plate of cookies in the heroine's house, he enters her house and takes those too, as well as her milk. Without asking. <br /><br />I think this behaviour was intended to be a humorous quirk to Jason's character, but I saw only pettiness and immaturity. Not someone I would want to know, and certainly not the attributes of a hero I have to admire for the romance to work. </span>

<div id="review_276339858" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/276339858" />
    <a title="Mimi Smith" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4884889-mimi-smith"><img alt="Mimi Smith" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1297016674p2/4884889.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/276339858?book_show_action=true">Feb 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mimi Smith" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mimi Smith" href="/user/show/4884889-mimi-smith">Mimi Smith</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4884889-mimi-smith?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer276339858" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1907519895520100378"><b>5 stars<br/><br/>It's been a long time since I've loved a book this much, so I'm spreading the word!</b><br/><br/>You know how they say "Don't judge a book by its cover"? Well, let's be honest:We all do. A pretty cover will get me to buy a book faster than a tempting blurb. I know, I know-it could be just me and my shallowness or I'm a plain old book cover snob, but it's a fact of life. Now, if this book wasn't recommended to me I never would've picked it up. <b>So, to all my GR friends who share my book cover predicament</b></span>
  <span id="freeText1907519895520100378" style="display:none"><b>5 stars<br /><br />It's been a long time since I've loved a book this much, so I'm spreading the word!</b><br /><br />You know how they say "Don't judge a book by its cover"? Well, let's be honest:We all do. A pretty cover will get me to buy a book faster than a tempting blurb. I know, I know-it could be just me and my shallowness or I'm a plain old book cover snob, but it's a fact of life. Now, if this book wasn't recommended to me I never would've picked it up. <b>So, to all my GR friends who share my book cover predicament, make an exception in this case 'cause this book rocks!</b><br /><br />What to say, what to say about this one...Well, firstly this book is funny as hell. It kind of reminds me of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/65137.Shelly_Laurenston" title="Shelly Laurenston" rel="nofollow noopener">Shelly Laurenston</a>'s books, only without the shifter part. You should be warned, if you don't know what that indicates, it means Jason is often childish, petulant, goofball charming, headstrong and OBSESSED WITH FOOD AND HALEY. He's simply adorable... And he's a teacher, too. So is Haley, to think of it.<br /><br /><i>“How dare you touch my cookies, you bastard!” Jason said in utter disgust before popping the cookie into his mouth and heading back to his house.<br />“Damn those looked good, too,” Brad grumbled.<br />Haley sighed. “Don’t worry I have a second plate on my counter.” The words were barely out of her mouth when Jason abruptly changed course and headed towards her house.<br />“Well, there was,” she said, watching Jason walk into her house like he owned it. A minute later he walked out of her house, carrying both plates and the gallon of milk she had in her fridge. He headed back to his house, but not before he glared at Brad. “You cookie thieving bastard,” they heard him mutter.<br />Brad rolled his eyes, chuckling. “And people wonder how I lost weight rooming with him in college.”<br /><br />"Jason rolled his eyes as he jumped to his feet. “I think calling any of them my girlfriends is a bit of an exaggeration. I rather you stick with referring to them as ‘the women who agreed to having a good time with no strings attached who got really pissed off at me when I got bored and left them for someone hotter.’”<br />“Wow, that’s a mouthful,” Brad murmured. “And surprising none of them has killed you yet."<br /><br />"I hate you," Haley mumbled, storming past him to grab a carriage.<br />"You love and adore me," Jason informed her as he deftly snagged her carriage away from her and headed towards the men's department."</i><br /><br />I can't remember the last time I've laughed this much while reading a book. There are a lot of ridiculous situations, but...It's great.<br /><br />I like Haley, too. I think she deals with the Hurricane That Is Jason admirably well. By that I mean she knows the way through his heart is through his stomach and that sometimes men are best ignored. She's a bit mousy, used to derision and snubs from her family, so being with a hot guy like Jason, wasn't something she thought would happen, but they came by it honestly. From enemies to buddies to a couple. YAY!!!!!!<br /><br />I loved these scenes...<br /><br /><i>"Soon he was picturing little girls with mischievous green eyes and pigtails asking him to play tea. Of course he'd bring real food to the tea party. None of that pretend food bullshit for his little girls.<br />By the time Haley had stopped for breakfast he'd been calmer about everything. He'd already decided to ignore that breakup nonsense. It was just ridiculous and he knew sooner or later Haley would realize that so they could get started on making their all girl baseball team."<br /><br />"This is kidnapping!" she sputtered in disbelief.<br />"No, it's not."<br />"Yes, it is!"<br />"Nope."<br />"What the hell would you call it?" she demanded, snatching his soda from him and finishing it off.<br />"A romantic getaway?"<br /></i><br /> <br />Now, I'll lay off the quotes, since I've been obsessively marking them in the book, lol. <br /><br />The only thing that bothered me a bit was his family's reaction to their dating. The You Don't Deserve Her was a bit too much.<br /><br /><b>HIGHLY RECOMMENDED!!!!!!!!!!!</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="1907519895520100378" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer10018475797612161216"><p>
  <b>Caution:You will laugh out loud!</b>

  <span id="freeText10018475797612161216" style="display:none"><p>
  <b>Caution:You will laugh out loud!</b>
</p><br><p>I mean it!</p><br><br>I hate reading funny books but this one was a random pick which turned out to be sooo good!<br><br>Enter,Jason<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433459i/872268.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He is 31 and definitely the biggest jackass on earth,or at least he seems to be.He is every householders' nightmare.We can see what a prick he is from Haley's eyes.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433459i/872269._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><p>

Can I have one?” a man she’d seen hundreds of times around Jason’s house asked, reaching out to take one. <br>“Back the fuck off!   <i>“How dare you touch my cookies, you bastard!” Jason said in utter disgust before popping the cookie into his mouth and heading back to his house. <br>“Damn those looked good, too,” Brad grumbled. <br>Haley sighed. “Don’t worry I have a second plate on my counter.” The words were barely out of her mouth when Jason abruptly changed course and headed towards her house. <br>“Well, there was,” she said, watching Jason walk into her house like he owned it. A minute later he walked out of her house, carrying both plates and the gallon of milk she had in her fridge. He headed back to his house, but not before he glared at Brad. “You cookie thieving bastard,” they heard him mutter. <br>Brad rolled his eyes, chuckling. “And people wonder how I lost weight rooming with him in college.”</i>
</b><br><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433459ra/872271.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Ps This is not a paranormal book.</span>

<div id="review_520338275" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/520338275" />
    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3072286-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415232045p2/3072286.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/520338275?book_show_action=true">Jan 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/3072286-beverly">Beverly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3072286-beverly?shelf=1-star">1-star</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer520338275&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer520338275" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13922399059896918682">Everything was cliché: she has a rich family that doesn’t appreciate her, the grandma is tough and she automatically approves of the ‘boyfriend’ even though she never has before, the son is the spitting image of the father, they <i>have</i> to wrestle in the mud to be close to each other upon meeting, he’s instantly turned on by her to the point of being unbearable, she’s amazing at foreplay even though she’s never done anything before, THEIR BEDROOM WINDOWS ARE LITERALLY LESS THAN TWO FEET APART FROM </span>
  <span id="freeText13922399059896918682" style="display:none">Everything was cliché: she has a rich family that doesn’t appreciate her, the grandma is tough and she automatically approves of the ‘boyfriend’ even though she never has before, the son is the spitting image of the father, they <i>have</i> to wrestle in the mud to be close to each other upon meeting, he’s instantly turned on by her to the point of being unbearable, she’s amazing at foreplay even though she’s never done anything before, THEIR BEDROOM WINDOWS ARE LITERALLY LESS THAN TWO FEET APART FROM EACH OTHER – how convenient, she has a confrontation with an old ex of his, he gets jealous about an old ex of hers, all the men who are not taken are deemed perverted assholes, all the girls but Haley are bitchy.<br /><br />He’s forced to use her shower, even though he lives next door, because they are trapped by bees – really? They surrounded the ENTIRE house? – and so he is forced to interact with each other where they discover they are not as bad as they thought they were and they go on to have the best friendship in the world. All so terrible.<br /><br />Haley was a total Mary-Sue. She’s a 29 year old virgin who has had, by what the book implies, literally hundreds of men trying to ask her out in her lifetime. I doubt not one of those men was good enough for Haley, the perfect prize. She’s apparently stunning, sexy, intelligent, sports-savvy, quirky, and humble. She’s every perfect characteristic packaged into one beautiful, lovely woman. Her only fault isn’t even about her, it’s the fact that she has a rich snobby family that doesn’t appreciate her. She’s made to seem like she was dealt with a hard life but she prospered despite her neglected childhood. She even refuses to receive help from people just because she needs to do things on her own. I mean, I understand wanting to do things on your own, but to literally pitch a fit because someone lied about how much a cabin they’re renting out for you cost? “Oh, no, she spent <i>way</i> over the $1000 limit I gave her! How dare she?”<br /><br />I hate this idea that a girl will only have sex with her one true love and that the man-whore will only settle for the innocent girl. Men are wild you can’t blame them for having sex with every model-like girl they meet and since girls are whores if they sleep with more than one guy then she needs to preserve her innocence in order to satisfy that one man. If you want to save yourself for marriage, fine by me whatever, but when they portray Haley as this completely innocent, good-natured girl and then couple that with her being a virgin, what does that really say? <br /><br />Jason is very immature, I find it hard to believe that he would ever be a good teacher, I’m surprised he hasn’t gotten fired. The food stuff was kind of entertaining in the beginning, but as soon as it was established that it was his <i>thing</i> it got annoying. He acts like a two year old yelling, “Mine!” and nearly crying whenever anyone goes near his precious brownies. Seriously?<br /><br />Even more so with the innocence and Mary-Sue stuff, Haley apparently doesn’t know that she’s beautiful and she’s unaware of all the attention she gets from guys. She’s so innocent she doesn’t even notice when men flirt with her. For a 29 year old, she seems pretty naïve. Also, Jason claiming to be a playboy and asserting over and over again the fact that he doesn’t let women sleep in his bed or cuddle with him? It was obvious they only put all that in there just to let Haley defy all of it and show that she was <i>special</i>! They don’t even really know each other and after claiming that she hated him for five years, they just go ahead and do it anyway! What kind of development is this? For people who were so adamant in their beliefs that they let them define them, they sure do break their own rules pretty quickly. <br /><br />I didn’t understand the whole ‘little grasshopper’ stuff. I get that he thinks it’s because he’s teaching her stuff, but what did he really do? All he did was invite her to a party where she branched out on her own. He left her alone for most of the time and it was only when he decided subconsciously that he wanted to sleep with her that he made himself her ‘coach’. She decided on her own to become less shy and he didn’t do anything regarding that. <br /><br />This idea that they’re such special soul-mates and whatever that they can’t even sleep if they’re not together???? Are you kidding me?? She literally says she hasn’t slept in five days because she <i>needs</i> Jason there with her. Can anyone, in real life, tell me if this has ever happened to you? I understand a day or two of having difficulty falling asleep because you’re sad about them, but to go DAYS without sleep because of it is just ridiculous. Going along with that, can you imagine if you moved houses and changed your workplace every time you broke up with a guy who lives/works nearby? Ridiculous. The entire ending was pretty dumb. It was just a bunch of groveling, stubbornness, and playing cat and mouse. They just went back and forth with their feelings and it got very annoying very fast. <br /><br /> <br />1/10 would not recommend.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13922399059896918682" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer1284137601990922227"><b>5 LMAO Stars</b><br/><br/>This is such a fun read! I told my friend I needed something light and she recommended this one, and it is perfect. <br/><br/>The story is about two neighbors who through little misunderstandings and some bad actions despise each other. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395196376ra/8964157.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Of course, once they are forced together one day and able to communicate things are cleared up. They immediately see they are perfect for each other and become best friends. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417475129ra/12391629.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Naturally their attraction for each other gets in the way and things escalate. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417475066i/12391625.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I liked </span>
  <span id="freeText1284137601990922227" style="display:none"><b>5 LMAO Stars</b><br><br>This is such a fun read! I told my friend I needed something light and she recommended this one, and it is perfect. <br><br>The story is about two neighbors who through little misunderstandings and some bad actions despise each other. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395196376ra/8964157.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Of course, once they are forced together one day and able to communicate things are cleared up. They immediately see they are perfect for each other and become best friends. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417475129ra/12391629.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Naturally their attraction for each other gets in the way and things escalate. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417475066i/12391625.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I liked how things didn't get too dramatic or angsty. Yes, this one was predictable, but I love Jason and Haley's little moments together. They fit together perfectly. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/655044.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This story is such a quick read, it will have you laughing out loud, and has some swoon worthy moments. I also loved my sexy scenes with Jason. <br><br>I recommend this one for when you are looking for something light and fun. </span>
  <a data-text-id="1284137601990922227" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_305104954" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/305104954" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/305104954?book_show_action=true">Apr 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=cute">cute</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=made-me-laugh">made-me-laugh</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer305104954" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13400873847314730387">3.5 stars. Rounding up because Jason is such a rock star. <br/><i>
  <blockquote>
    <b>She quietly said good night, rolled her eyes as Jason mumbled, "I love you" to his brownies, and headed off to the bathroom.</b>
  </blockquote>
</i><br/>I picked up <i>Playing for Keeps</i> because it was getting some attention and I was curious to see why a seemingly unnoticeable book (have you seen the cover?) was starting to cause a stir.<br/><br/><b>What I was expecting :</b> Neighbors who don't get along spend half of a book torturing the living daylights out of each other </span>
  <span id="freeText13400873847314730387" style="display:none">3.5 stars. Rounding up because Jason is such a rock star. <br /><i>
  <blockquote>
    <b>She quietly said good night, rolled her eyes as Jason mumbled, "I love you" to his brownies, and headed off to the bathroom.</b>
  </blockquote>
</i><br />I picked up <i>Playing for Keeps</i> because it was getting some attention and I was curious to see why a seemingly unnoticeable book (have you seen the cover?) was starting to cause a stir.<br /><br /><b>What I was expecting :</b> Neighbors who don't get along spend half of a book torturing the living daylights out of each other before they finally realize their attraction.<br /><br /><b>What really happened :</b> Neighbors torture each other for a <i>very</i> brief period of time, before the rest of the book has them exploring a friends-turned-lovers scenario.<br /><br />While I had hoped for a lot more "neighbor from hell" action, I was not disappointed with the turn of events. Granted, it would have been a riot to read an entire book of neighbors sabotaging each other (if you guys know of one, shoot me a rec, please)...but I can honestly say that this was a fun read, regardless of how it turned out!<br /><br /><b>This book does prove that I am the queen of double standards.</b> I have a statement on my profile saying that it's up the author to convince me to buy into something I wouldn't normally like about a book. I'm happy to report that this author had me buying everything hook, line and sinker.<br /><br /><b>Drama :</b> As much as I enjoy reading a good drama-fest, I usually find myself complaining that it's been done in such a manner which is way too over-the-top. PFK is an example of how to write drama into a book without taking it to a point where you want to strangle the characters.<br /><br /><b>Nicknames :</b> Again, this is another big turnoff for me. Outside of VA's endearing use of Roza and Dimka, I'm usually not a fan. I know that not everyone loved the use of "Grasshopper" in this book but I found it cute and personal. Maybe because of this : <i>She glared over her shoulder at him. "I'm not going to call you Mr. Miyagi you know."<br />"Yes you will, but that's not important at the moment."</i><br /><br /><b>Epilogues :</b> Rarely, are they necessary. In the case of PFK, I appreciated the followup.<br /><br />I enjoyed the book so much that I didn't even mind a few typos. In fact, one of them even added to my enjoyment. How could you not laugh at : <i>Fists of Furry</i>?<br /><br />Love story aside, Jason is the real reason to read PFK. His love for food is probably even more entertaining than his love for Hayley.<br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"You never brought me to a buffet restaurant at home," she pointed out.<br />Jason mumbled something.<br />"What?" she asked.<br />"I said, I've been banned," he grumbled unhappily. "It's all political," he sniffed.<br />"Uh huh...and your father?" she asked.<br />"He's been banned since 1995," Jason said with a shrug. "In two years the ban in Las Vegas will be lifted. We're planning a big trip," he said.<br />"You've been banned from Las Vegas?"<br />"Not from Las Vegas, just from all the buffets."<br />"All the buffets?" There had to be hundreds of buffets in Las Vegas.<br />"I guess they had a meeting or something. As I said before, it's all political."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13400873847314730387" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_867365670" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/867365670" />
    <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish"><img alt="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1398981306p2/1113032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/867365670?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="user" itemprop="url" name="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish">UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=first-in-series-trilogy-duet">first-in-series-trilogy-duet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=own-have-read">own-have-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=author-r-l-mathewson">author-r-l-mathewson</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=format-kindle-or-kindle-compatible">format-kindle-or-kindle-compatible</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=must-read-author">must-read-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=virginal-heroine">virginal-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=must-reread">must-reread</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=4-stars">4-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=must-read-series">must-read-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=funny-sexy-romantic">funny-sexy-romantic</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer867365670" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18142796798971182540"><br/><b>
  <i>4 ‘I giggled, I snickered, and fanned myself' stars!!!</i>
</b><br/><br/><i>Playing for Keeps</i> is the first book in R.L. Mathewson’s <i>Neighbor from Hell</i> series and one hell of a funny story. <br/><br/><b>Description…</b><br/><br/>Done with being the world's biggest pushover, Haley decides that things are going to change starting with the aggravating neighbor who has too much charm and not enough restraint. What she didn't expect was to be sucked into his world, but Haley has a game plan and she won't let herself forget just what the bad boy </span>
  <span id="freeText18142796798971182540" style="display:none"><br /><b>
  <i>4 ‘I giggled, I snickered, and fanned myself' stars!!!</i>
</b><br /><br /><i>Playing for Keeps</i> is the first book in R.L. Mathewson’s <i>Neighbor from Hell</i> series and one hell of a funny story. <br /><br /><b>Description…</b><br /><br />Done with being the world's biggest pushover, Haley decides that things are going to change starting with the aggravating neighbor who has too much charm and not enough restraint. What she didn't expect was to be sucked into his world, but Haley has a game plan and she won't let herself forget just what the bad boy next door is capable of. <br /><br />The last thing Jason expected was for his little shy neighbor to go Rambo on him over some ruined flowers. After he decides to take her under his wing he can't help but notice that she fits very nicely in his life. Now the only thing left is to convince her that this is anything but a game.<br /><br /><b>My review...</b><br /><br />I picked this up back in the days of Fictionwise and their 60% off sales but never got around to reading it because I wasn’t in the mood for a paranormal romance about demons living next door. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>**snort**</b>
</i> <br /><br />Man, oh man! I wish I had paid closer attention to what the book was about because I’ve been missing out on some seriously good times!! <br /><br />Like I said, for some reason I thought this was, literally, a story about demon neighbors. Don't bother asking why, because I haven't a clue, but yeah, I assumed this was a PNR. And although Jason is definitely a neighbor from hell, it’s not the literal kind of hell. He’s just a pain in the ass. The kind of neighbor who has you thinking of selling your home, or burning his down. Prison time starts looking good if it means ridding the world of him and his annoying, loud, friends.<br /><br />After realizing that this is <i>not</i> a PNR, I was anticipating a light, fun read and yeah, I got that, but there’s something more about <i>Playing for Keeps;</i> a connection between myself and the characters I can't explain and wasn't expecting. At first I thought I’d feel nothing more than ‘meh’ for Jason, but by the end of the book I adored him! He and his family are just hysterical and I laughed out loud more than a few times at their banter. And the sex scenes? Holy hell hot!<br /><br /><b>The bottom line…</b><br /><br />This isn’t a deep or compelling novel, but it’s sexy, romantic, funny and thoroughly entertaining. Even as I sit here writing this review I’m grinning from ear to ear as I recall some of Haley and Jason’s antics, and those of Jason’s goofy friends. <br /><br />I’ve already downloaded book 2, <i>Perfection</i> and can’t wait to dive in!</span>
  <a data-text-id="18142796798971182540" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

A lot of my friends rated PLAYING FOR KEEPS very highly. Now, I'm questioning that, as I couldn't find anything that really called to me about this book. Haley and Jason are both incredibly immature. The book starts out as an enemies-to-lovers romance but they get over being enemies really quickly and then it becomes a friends-to-lovers romance instead. I felt like their reactions made them feel like high school students instead of adults in their twenties, and the "humor" in this book felt similarly juvenile.<br><br><br><br>Since I didn't get very far in, I don't have a lot to say about PLAYING FOR KEEPS except that 1) this book is definitely not a keeper, 2) it is boring AF, and 3) thank God I didn't pay money for this, or I'd be super angry about the waste.<br><br><br><br>1 star</span>

<div id="review_532817409" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/532817409" />
    <a title="Susanne " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7179798-susanne"><img alt="Susanne " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1511902036p2/7179798.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/532817409?book_show_action=true">Feb 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Susanne " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Susanne " href="/user/show/7179798-susanne">Susanne </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/11476515-playing-for-keeps">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7179798-susanne?shelf=genre-other-romance">genre-other-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer532817409" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14197384893289635919">Gah! This book was so freaking amazing and then it had to fall into the CR-trap. Yes, I made it up right now. Beware, the second part of this review will contain mild spoilers. I will let you know when.<br/><br/><b>The first part.</b> So incredibly funny! I laughed so much on the train that the people around me thought I was crazy. It was brilliant!<br/><br/><b>Haley.</b> Sweet bookish heroine who is done with being a pushover. <br/><br/><i>She was always the shy girl with her nose buried in a book, hoping no one would notice her.</i><br/><br/><i>Who knew th</i></span>
  <span id="freeText14197384893289635919" style="display:none">Gah! This book was so freaking amazing and then it had to fall into the CR-trap. Yes, I made it up right now. Beware, the second part of this review will contain mild spoilers. I will let you know when.<br /><br /><b>The first part.</b> So incredibly funny! I laughed so much on the train that the people around me thought I was crazy. It was brilliant!<br /><br /><b>Haley.</b> Sweet bookish heroine who is done with being a pushover. <br /><br /><i>She was always the shy girl with her nose buried in a book, hoping no one would notice her.</i><br /><br /><i>Who knew there was a little tigress beneath all that cuteness.</i><br /><br /><b>Jason.</b> The neighbor from hell. He makes Haley his project and find a best friend. And they fall in love. It is a beautiful enemies-to-friends-to-lovers tale. Ebony hair, ocean blue eyes and chiseled good look. Swoon alert! And Jason loves food. This book will make you hungry.<br /><br /><b>The good.</b> Funny and sweet, and I loved hanging with them. The friendship is adorable, and even more so how oblivious they are to the fact that they've fallen in love.<br /><br /><b>The bad.</b> Haley is a virgin. She is waiting for the one. So obviously, this is a very tame CR by any standards. And the way this is used as a plot device didn't work for me.<br /><br /><b>The ugly.</b> Here it comes. The CR-trap. Gah! Everything is moving along nicely, you love the hero and the heroine and they are beginning to realize that they love each other. And boom! A silly misunderstanding. Jason was a complete jerk and acted out of character. Haley gets upset. I get it. She refuses to talk to him. He tries. He gives up. She tries. He refuses. Boom. In one page we get back to loving each other - and yes we now know after being apart for several weeks, yelling and fighting nasty that we are going to get married right away. Yes, that's how I wanted my proposal to go down. NOT! They have the most dysfunctional fight ever - but we are getting married now. Sorry for the rant. But why ruin something beautiful with a childish out-of-character fight?<br /><br /><b>In the end.</b> A beautiful epilogue that almost made it up to me. I would give the first part five shining stars, the last 25 percent one sad star and the epilogue four blooming stars again. If you can look past the CR-trap, then I really recommend it!</span>
  <a data-text-id="14197384893289635919" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer7222409700591108232">Always a glutton for punishment, Haley Blaine believes she can tolerate anything her jerk of a neighbor can dish out. After five years of his antics, she has had enough and flips out on him and has no plans in holding back her unleashed fury, well that is until she finds out the real reason he was tearing up her garden.<br/><br/>Jason Bradford loves women, just doesn't love them enough to start a relationship with him. After five years of getting the cold shoulder from his neighbor, he is delightfully sur</span>
  <span id="freeText7222409700591108232" style="display:none">Always a glutton for punishment, Haley Blaine believes she can tolerate anything her jerk of a neighbor can dish out. After five years of his antics, she has had enough and flips out on him and has no plans in holding back her unleashed fury, well that is until she finds out the real reason he was tearing up her garden.<br /><br />Jason Bradford loves women, just doesn't love them enough to start a relationship with him. After five years of getting the cold shoulder from his neighbor, he is delightfully surprised to find out she is a baseball fan, cooks sinfully delicious goodies, and a total blast to hang with. As a unique friendship develops, both Jason and Haley find themselves dating each other without actually dating one another, only time will tell if it will develop into something more.<br /><br />I thought this was a huge surprise, it is funny, cute, and has just enough surprises to keep me from putting it down. Jason has an obsessively unhealthy addiction to food, which adds several extremely funny moments in the book. Fantastic read, I would not have looked at it twice, but found it in the you might also like section. Glad I did.<br /><br />**Reread because I had read Perfection. So here is the head scratcher for me, in this book they are both teachers. In the next book, Perfection Jason works for his dad's construction company? Althought he may just be helping out but I was kind of boggled on this part. There are some pretty funny moments in this book that I forgot about.</span>

<div id="review_871183720" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/871183720" />
    <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27276528-liz"><img alt="✰ Liz ✰ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451097545p2/27276528.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/871183720?book_show_action=true">Mar 03, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✰ Liz ✰ " href="/user/show/27276528-liz">✰ Liz ✰ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/20695552-playing-for-keeps">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=hillarious">hillarious</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=sugary-sweet">sugary-sweet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=audioread">audioread</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=high-angst-alert">high-angst-alert</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=not-what-i-expected">not-what-i-expected</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer871183720" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3307564067101991482"><b>“If she tried to leave without him he would burn her house down, plain and simple.” </b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436046395i/15412082.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Playing for Keeps is a light hearted modern romance with an abundance of satire and a great deal of tongue and cheek humor.<br/><br/>For the past five years, Haley has been living next door to “the neighbor from Hell”. Haley is a "rule follower” with an abundance of “polish" and sophistication. Jason is a sporadic “free spirit”. Needless to say, the two are quite opposite.<br/><br/>Haley and Jason don’t get along. Haley has worked d</span>
  <span id="freeText3307564067101991482" style="display:none"><b>“If she tried to leave without him he would burn her house down, plain and simple.” </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436046395i/15412082.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Playing for Keeps is a light hearted modern romance with an abundance of satire and a great deal of tongue and cheek humor.<br><br>For the past five years, Haley has been living next door to “the neighbor from Hell”. Haley is a "rule follower” with an abundance of “polish" and sophistication. Jason is a sporadic “free spirit”. Needless to say, the two are quite opposite.<br><br>Haley and Jason don’t get along. Haley has worked diligently to avoid Jason. He is constantly having loud parties and partaking in drunken shenanigans with his friends. Then one night, he is pulling up her tulips and she realizes she has had enough. She confronts him and this is when everything begins to transform.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436047479i/15412239._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>“Hey! Stop that!” he demanded as he leaned over her to grab a hold of her hands. “Get off me!” she snapped, digging faster. “I wouldn’t be on you if you weren’t on my damn property!”</b><br><br> In addition to neighbors, they are also teachers that teach at the same school. The combination of the proximity of the two and the fact that they both compliment each other so perfectly prompts Haley and Jason to become friends. You know the age old saying really does apply in most cases...opposites do indeed attract! Haley bakes for Jason. (And Jason loves to eat!) Jason begins to influence Haley as he helps her out of her shell. They begin to hang out, cuddle, and just become best friends. It doesn’t take long for things to transform into more than friendship between the two. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436046395i/15412083.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The two share a very comfortable and yet humorous romance. This is most definitely a friends to lovers story with a flair of “war of the roses”. Written in dual POV we are able to peek into the minds of both of these main characters. The dialogue is truly hilarious and the steam was off the charts. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436046395i/15412084.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Overall, I recommend Playing for Keeps for readers that enjoy a light romantic comedy. There were many tender moments and moments that made me laugh. Often, I did find Haley and Jason to be very immature. If you take on this read, just be prepared for a little eye rolling. However, if you are able to suspend reality for the sake of enjoyment then by all means dive right in. I will add that the epilogue was very tender and sweet. Overall, a truly enjoyable read. <br><br> <b>I listened to this book on audible.com!</b><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="3307564067101991482" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer2043757195778603824">I am sorry but this book was beyond boring... Maybe, I shouldn't have rated it because I dropped it at page 100. Looked at the last 2 or 3 pages and I didn't have the strength to read the epilogue...<br/><br/>The story was meant to be humorous, I never - even once- smiled, let alone laugh...<br/><br/>By the way, how can a coward and introvert woman change in the blink of an eye and become this confident and fun girl?<br/><br/>How can a 30 year-old guy act so childishly? Not cute, no not cute, very annoying... There was nothi</span>
  <span id="freeText2043757195778603824" style="display:none">I am sorry but this book was beyond boring... Maybe, I shouldn't have rated it because I dropped it at page 100. Looked at the last 2 or 3 pages and I didn't have the strength to read the epilogue...<br /><br />The story was meant to be humorous, I never - even once- smiled, let alone laugh...<br /><br />By the way, how can a coward and introvert woman change in the blink of an eye and become this confident and fun girl?<br /><br />How can a 30 year-old guy act so childishly? Not cute, no not cute, very annoying... There was nothing charming about him.<br /><br />The way their relationship began, the way it proceeded ... oh, it was so meaningless, so boring for me...<br /><br />I couldn't stand it and even though I hate dropping a book, I dropped this one.<br /><br />I didn't feel the angst and tension between them at first, then I didn't feel the romance/love between them either. It was never fun. I don't know you guys, but I would never like to be called "My little grasshopper"... Yuck!<br /><br />And the writing was bad - it never flowed...<br /><br />Sorry, but even if I went on and read all of it, I doubt I would say anything nicer. And if you can't continue reading a book, you shouldn't really...</span>
  <a data-text-id="2043757195778603824" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_284442255" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/284442255" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/284442255?book_show_action=true">Feb 26, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer284442255" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17708076239867050743">I really liked this book a lot. It was the PERFECT fluff read for me. It was well written, with characters I really cared about, lots of adorably cute and funny moments, no heart-breaking moments, no damaged or tortured characters, didn't make me cry at any point, really really adorable HEAs, and not super long reads. I read this book and its sequel in 4 hours. It was the perfect way to spend a sunny afternoon.<br/><br/>I love the way their relationship developed. It was perfectly paced. Fast enough that </span>
  <span id="freeText17708076239867050743" style="display:none">I really liked this book a lot. It was the PERFECT fluff read for me. It was well written, with characters I really cared about, lots of adorably cute and funny moments, no heart-breaking moments, no damaged or tortured characters, didn't make me cry at any point, really really adorable HEAs, and not super long reads. I read this book and its sequel in 4 hours. It was the perfect way to spend a sunny afternoon.<br /><br />I love the way their relationship developed. It was perfectly paced. Fast enough that I never felt that the story dragged, but not so fast that it felt rushed. Literally the entire point of the story is about two people who fall in love and how they get to their HEA. No complications, no external drama, no bad guy, just a love story. It was EXACTLY what I wanted. Looking forward to reading more by this author.<br /><br />I gotta say the grasshopper thing was ADORABLE!!!! Jason was an awesome hero and Hayley was a cute heroine (nice to read one that didnt annoy me) :)<br /><br />4.5+ stars.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17708076239867050743" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/278576030" />
    <a title="Karla" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3024056-karla"><img alt="Karla" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1324910771p2/3024056.jpg" /></a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780983212539" href="/book/show/11255461-playing-for-keeps">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Karla by: </span>
      Searock and Steffi

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer278576030" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12304742133304172026">The ideal blend of romance, humor, angst, and spice! I loved everything about this book. Jason and Haley’s first interaction, their friendship that becomes more, the falling out, the reconciling, and lordy lordy their time between the sheets was steamy and sensual. The writing is wonderful, plenty of witty dialogue, and it included a delightful array of amusing secondary characters. <br/><br/>It’s the perfect length; it was enough story that you’re committed to the characters, yet the plot is not overwhel</span>
  <span id="freeText12304742133304172026" style="display:none">The ideal blend of romance, humor, angst, and spice! I loved everything about this book. Jason and Haley’s first interaction, their friendship that becomes more, the falling out, the reconciling, and lordy lordy their time between the sheets was steamy and sensual. The writing is wonderful, plenty of witty dialogue, and it included a delightful array of amusing secondary characters. <br /><br />It’s the perfect length; it was enough story that you’re committed to the characters, yet the plot is not overwhelming. I felt very much at ease with Jason and Haley’s relationship, it was comfortable and developed rather nicely. The time they spent together as buddies made me adore them even more. Jason’s love affair with food had me rolling my eyes and laughing out loud, and Haley’s transformation from shy schoolteacher to the brawling grasshopper with her “fits of fury” was a picture I could not get out of my head. I wanted them to be together as more than just friends, but the pace that was set for them to get there fit the characters and their circumstances. At one point I felt rather annoyed with Haley and her stubbornness when it came to forgiving Jason, yes he could be a jerk, but the good in him outweighed the bad. When the realization hits her that she might lose him forever, she uses tactics that is reminiscent of Jason when we first met him…. his grasshopper has learned well! <br /><br />I didn’t want Jason and Haley's story to end, I wanted more time with this adorable couple, but all good things must come to an end. Alas, it does, but R. L. Mathewson gives us a satisfying epilogue that warmed my heart and put a huge smile on my face.<br /><br /><br /><b>We are currently having a Giveaway at Swept Away By Romance-R.L. Mathewson is giving away ALL of her published books to 2 very lucky winners (ends on February 23, 2012)</b> <br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/">http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/</a><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12304742133304172026" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_887945053" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/887945053" />
    <a title="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth"><img alt="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487525094p2/13870608.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/887945053?book_show_action=true">Mar 21, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" href="/user/show/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth">Jo ★The Book Sloth★</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer887945053" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4770838880501839640"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395566874i/9014747.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I was very surprised when I realized how funny this book was. I had a huge smile on my face most of the time and I can't count the times I laughed out loud. It's not something that happens a lot with contemporary romance since the dark and angsty are in fashion so I'm very happy for this.<br/><br/>The characters and the writing reminded me very much of one of my favorite authors <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/65137.Shelly_Laurenston' title='Shelly Laurenston' rel='nofollow noopener'>Shelly Laurenston</a>. At some point I was beginning to think that they are the same person. I visited the authors page and I wasn't</span>
  <span id="freeText4770838880501839640" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395566874i/9014747.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was very surprised when I realized how funny this book was. I had a huge smile on my face most of the time and I can't count the times I laughed out loud. It's not something that happens a lot with contemporary romance since the dark and angsty are in fashion so I'm very happy for this.<br><br>The characters and the writing reminded me very much of one of my favorite authors <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/65137.Shelly_Laurenston" title="Shelly Laurenston" rel="nofollow noopener">Shelly Laurenston</a>. At some point I was beginning to think that they are the same person. I visited the authors page and I wasn't too surprised to read this...<br><br><i>Influences: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/1395810.G_A__Aiken" title="G.A. Aiken" rel="nofollow noopener">G.A. Aiken</a></i><br><br>G.A. Aiken is a pen name for SL. Anyway... It comes as little surprise to me that I loved the crazy behaviours and dialogs.<br><br><b>
  <u>The couple</u>
</b><br><br><b>Jason</b> was hilarious... I have no other word to describe him. He was arrogant, selfish(not with the heroine, with everyone else), stubborn and he had an addiction to food. He was like a tasmanian devil with the food and he didn't share. His family was equaly crazy and had the same appetite. I have a thing for crazy characters so I loved him.<br><br><b>
  <i>“How dare you touch my cookies, you bastard!” Jason said in utter disgust before popping the cookie into his mouth and heading back to his house.<br>“Damn those looked good, too,” Brad grumbled.<br>Haley sighed. “Don’t worry I have a second plate on my counter.” The words were barely out of her mouth when Jason abruptly changed course and headed towards her house.<br>“Well, there was,” she said, watching Jason walk into her house like he owned it. A minute later he walked out of her house, carrying both plates and the gallon of milk she had in her fridge. He headed back to his house, but not before he glared at Brad. “You cookie thieving bastard,” they heard him mutter.<br>Brad rolled his eyes, chuckling. “And people wonder how I lost weight rooming with him in college.” </i>
</b><br><br><b>Haley</b> was an awkward girl. She was used to being the doormat and having people walk all over her. She was also insanely hot but she didn't realize it. I liked Haley. She was quiet and easy-going but once you got to know her you realized that she was smart and funny. She was also a genuinely nice person. Oh, and she loved her Yankees.<br><br>I would have given this book a 5* rating but at some point it dragged a bit. Jason did a shitty thing, Haley got scared, they both behaved like idiots. I get that there has to be a story but it wasn't as nice as the rest of the book.<br><br>I still loved it!<br><br><b>
  <i>"For god sake, Jason, I dumped you!" she snapped, feeling the last thread of patience snap.<br>She looked up in the rearview mirror when he didn't say anything for a minute only to find his frowning. Finally he shook his head. "No, I think I would have remembered that."</i>
</b></span>

<div id="review_2895093482" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2895093482" />
    <a title="Syndi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1656405-syndi"><img alt="Syndi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1560317991p2/1656405.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2895093482?book_show_action=true">Jul 28, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Syndi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Syndi" href="/user/show/1656405-syndi">Syndi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2895093482" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2166857998037695235">This is my first read by Miss Mathewson. I listen to the audiobook because in Goodreads the review is awsome. Many said funny as hell. Wanting something fun for my Sunday read, i started listening to it. <br/><br/>It is funny. Very funny that i cracked a laugh while listening to it. But then, there are a lot of things i do not understand. <br/><br/>1. The age of the character. Early 30's. Both are teacher. But their communication and their banter is more suitable for 18 years old. <br/><br/>2. The push and pull between the c</span>
  <span id="freeText2166857998037695235" style="display:none">This is my first read by Miss Mathewson. I listen to the audiobook because in Goodreads the review is awsome. Many said funny as hell. Wanting something fun for my Sunday read, i started listening to it. <br /><br />It is funny. Very funny that i cracked a laugh while listening to it. But then, there are a lot of things i do not understand. <br /><br />1. The age of the character. Early 30's. Both are teacher. But their communication and their banter is more suitable for 18 years old. <br /><br />2. The push and pull between the characters at the end of the story is too much and too dragging. Yes i do love a good grooveling, but not that many push and pull. <br /><br />3. The issue with Hailey's virginity. Is this element necessary?? Can it be another different issue that is more suitable for someone in early 30's?<br /><br />4. The chemistry between the characters. For 3 months they have platonic sleeping arrangement. So before they met, both of them unable to sleep?? And platonic for 3 months??? I really do not understand this. <br /><br />Overall i do enjoy this book. It is serves the purpose to me as a fun read. It is really funny. <br /><br />3 stars</span>
  <a data-text-id="2166857998037695235" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('7gnoSdagZp1rHmH3b8EAX+V6qWwX5uyjQ2rZbzVLE+hqTHWIvKlhuk6IGQF+xotEediK0wo+ds9q6ltPaJhlyQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('J/pwLKVjWDSloFUjFnjANVmQdUVjmiYZ27lJG2Qp+tyjv+3tz2pfE4A2LdUHf0suxTJW+n5CvHXyOcs7OfqM/Q==')})
  }

Thanks to paper-thin walls and the guy\'s athletic prowess, she can hear <\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText15923681720919487659\" style=\"display:none\">The first night after Caroline moves into her fantastic new San Francisco apartment, she realizes she\'s gaining an intimate knowledge of her new neighbor\'s nocturnal adventures. Thanks to paper-thin walls and the guy\'s athletic prowess, she can hear not just his bed banging against the wall but the ecstatic response of what seems (as loud night after loud night goes by) like an endless parade of women. And since Caroline is currently on a self-imposed dating hiatus, and her neighbor is clearly lethally attractive to women, she finds her fantasies keep her awake even longer than the noise. So when the wallbanging threatens to literally bounce her out of bed, Caroline, clad in sexual frustration and a pink baby-doll nightie, confronts Simon Parker, her heard-but-never-seen neighbor. The tension between them is as thick as the walls are thin, and the results just as mixed. <div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer11919379644878143029">New York Times Bestselling author, R.L. Mathewson was born in Massachusetts. She’s known for her humor, quick wit and ability to write relatable characters. She currently has several paranormal and contemporary romance series published including the Neighbor from Hell series. <br/><br/>Growing up, R.L. Mathewson was a painfully shy bookworm. After high school she attended college, worked as a bellhop, fast </span>
  <span id="freeText11919379644878143029" style="display:none">New York Times Bestselling author, R.L. Mathewson was born in Massachusetts. She’s known for her humor, quick wit and ability to write relatable characters. She currently has several paranormal and contemporary romance series published including the Neighbor from Hell series. <br /><br />Growing up, R.L. Mathewson was a painfully shy bookworm. After high school she attended college, worked as a bellhop, fast food cook, and a museum worker until she decided to take an EMT course. Working as an EMT helped her get over her shyness as well as left her with some fond memories and some rather disturbing ones that from time to time show up in one of her books. <br /><br />Today, R.L. Mathewson is the single mother of two children that keep her on her toes. She has a bit of a romance novel addiction as well as a major hot chocolate addiction and on a perfect day, she combines the two. <br /><br />In 2019/2020, R.L. Mathewson will be publishing Devastated, the first Anger Management novel, Tall, Dark &amp; Furious, the 6th installment to the Pyte/Sentinel series, Irresistible, the long anticipated novel for the Neighbor from Hell Series as well as many more books throughout the year, paranormals, contemporaries, and YAs. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11919379644878143029" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

A minute later he walked out of her house, carrying both plates and the gallon of milk she had in her fridge. He headed back to his house, but not before he glared at Brad. “You cookie thieving bastard,” they heard him mutter. <br />Brad rolled his eyes, chuckling. “And people wonder how I lost weight rooming with him in college.&rdquo;</span>
